'di rnams sku mdog gcig tu ma nges so// 'di kun zhing bsnol ma'i khri la bzhugs so// bdud rtsi lha mo de rnams kyang // phyag mtshan rdo rje bum pa 'dzin/ sku mdog dmar po pad+ma'i gdan la bzhugs so// bcom ldan 'das seng ge'i khri nyi zla brtsegs pa'i gdan la sku lus glang po che'i cha byad du sprul nas mdzad// yang sprul chen mo seng ge lcam dral dang / stag lcam dral dang / wa lcam dral dang / spyang mo lcam dral dang / bya rgod lcam dral dang / kang ka lcam dral dang / bya rog lcam dral dang / 'ug pa lcam dral dang / 'di dag kun gyi ye shes sprul pa'o// pha bang lcam dral dang / zer mo mo dom gyi mgo / bdud rtsi sngon mo rin chen chu srin mgo// zhi ba sngo skya bam chen snying 'byin stag gi mgo// be con nag mo bam chen thod rlon khra yi mgo// srin mo nag mo bam chen rgyu zhags wa yi mgo / za byed nag mo bam chen snying 'byin stag gi mgo / dga' byed nag mo khong chen bgegs rgyal bya rgod mgo / khrag 'thung dmar mo rdo rje dbyug dung dmar rta'i mgo / gcig pu dkar dmar nam mkha' lding gi mgo / yid 'phrog dmar ser bzhis bsdus byi za khyi yi mgo / grub ma dkar dmar sad ma byi za pu shud mgo / rlung mo dmar ser ro za rdo rje sha ba'i mgo / gsod byed skya ljang bam chen rde'u chung skye ka'i mgo / me mo dmar ser mo srag rgyu 'dren skyin gyi mgo / phag mo ljang nag rtse sbyin rlon dmar phag gi mgo / dmar mo ljang sngon bdud rtsi'i khrag 'thung khra yi mgo / sna chen ljang nag bam chen longs spyod ba lang mgo / grub mo ljang ser bdud rtsi b+han dmar sbrul gyi mgo / phag mo lcags kyu phu tra rdo rje khu byug ma/ ra ni ser mo rgyu zhags ra yi mgo / bum sna dmar mo lcags de nyid bstan pa yin// sangs rgyas byang chub bde chen po// gang gis chud pas rdzogs sangs rgyas// sems can mchog gi ston byed na// de nyid sangs rgyas byang chub 'grub// de nas bcom ldan gcig 'dus nas// rab tu spro ba'i spyan gdangs nas// zhabs dang zhabs kyis gnon pa yis// sdud cing 'dor ba 'jug par mdzad// g.yas dang g.yon gyi phyag gnyis kyis// brjid pa'i rtse mo mtha' nas dgrol// cung zad ma dang / 'di rnams kyi sku mdog ni sna tshogs pa'o// phyag na mtshon cha sna tshogs pa'o// drag byed bdag pos sgrol bar byed pa'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das dpal he ru kas sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo pa'i 'brug sgra chen po ldir// mgo gsum po la lcags sder can// mi sha za zhing bdud dpung 'joms// bltas pas bdud rnams tshig byed cing // klu yi khyim rnams rab tu 'joms// rab tu mi srun 'di dag ni// 'di yang dpal gyi pho nya ste// las rnams thams cad grub par gyis// mtshan dang dpe byad gnyis las 'phros// mgyogs pa mgyogs ma'i pho nyar ldan// glog 'gyu ma dang 'dra bar grags// chos nyid khyab pas 'phro ba ni// hU~M dang phaT kyi sgra sgrogs shing // bskal pa'i 'brug sgra chen po bzhin// kun kyang mgyogs ma rlung dang mtshungs// mig gsum yo la lcags sder can// mgo gsum po la rkang gsum pa// song ba yi// khro bo thams cad nges par 'jig // na mo byi tsir b+h+yo// ha ha ru lu ru lu b+h+yo// mgo brgyad po la rkang brgyad po// lag pa brgyad la mig kyang brgyad// lag pa brgyad ni rdo rje 'dzin// rta mgrin gnas kyang nges par 'joms// mgo drug po la rkang drug po// lag pa drug ni rgyud drug gcod// rkang pa gsum ni phur bu 'dril// g.yon pa gsum ni gtor ma sbyin// gang nas gang du 'gro ba'i tshe// rkang pa lcags phur rab tu drag // 'od zer dud kas reg pa ni// tshangs pa'i gnas kyang rab tu 'jig // lag pa g.yon pas bskyod pa ni// phra men 'khor bcas ral par 'bar// lcags kyus dgra sta rab thogs shing // zhing chen yan lag 'dzin pa 'phro// byang gi phyogs nas 'byung ba ni// lcags kyi khyi ste rkang gsum po// lcags kyi lus la nyi ma'i mig // spu ni lcags kyu bsregs pa 'dra// bang ni gnag la sbrul gyis brgyan// ral pa gnag cing mche ba gnag // mig kyang gnag la lag nag po// mgyogs kyang rlung gis bskyod du med// 'di dag pho nya'i mchog yin pas// las rnams thams cad grub par gyis// long ba rgyab sbrel phyi ma nang // maM sa za zhing ri lu sgrol// mig kyang med la cang mi smra// yang na lag pa sbrel te 'gro// 'di yang khro bo'i pho nya ste// las rnams thams cad grub par byed// yang dag pa'i bden du ngas par rig par bya'o// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shin tu gsang ba he ru ka'i rol pa las rdo rje pho nya'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis nyid kyi bcur nges nas/ de ni phye byang ngo bstan te gses nas bshad pa/ de la lung gsum ni zhi gnas mi rtog dngos po mkha' khyab 'dra// lhag mthong ma rmongs gza' skar mkha' la bkram// gdod bcas don dang gyi mtshan// tshul khrims ting 'dzin shes rab gsum dang ldan// pad+ma 'dam skyes ma chags thugs rjes spyod// tshul khrims pha rol phyin pa'i ngang du bstan// mi zad par ldan sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin// ral gri ye shes thugs rje mtha' gnyis gcod// rtse gcig ting 'dzin gnyis las brtson 'grus mdzad// dgra sta zhags pa la sogs phyag mtshan rnams// rang gnyer las kyi brda tsam chos sku rtogs par bstan// de la 'di man chad che mchog yon tan gyi lung gis spyir dril te bshad pa ni/ yon tan gyi brjid la phrin las kyi rngom sum cu rtsa drug bstan pa ni de la sku'i rngom pa bzhi la nam mkha' ri mo phyag rgyar rngom/ cir yang 'gyur bzhi bzhugs tshul rngom/ zil gyis gnon pa'i gdan rngom/ tsham ngam chen po'i stobs rngom pa dang bzhi'o// de yang kun rdzob rang bzhin med pa la nam mkha' la sprin da ba'i tshul dang / lha dang 'phags pa tshangs pa dang / smon lam cir yang 'gyur ba'i bzhugs thabs kyi tshul dang / srid pa'i 'khor lo zil gyis gnon pa dri med pad+ma nyi zla 'od yon tan rtags de gdan khri'i tshul dang / stobs chen bcu'i tshul dang / rnam pa ni 'og nas 'chad do// gsung gi rngom bzhi la hom lnga 'brel par 'byung ba'i zhal rngom/ zla gam cir yang 'gyur ba'i ljags rngom/ skye shi rtsa ba gcod pa'i tshems rngom/ gsung sgra 'brug ltar sgrogs pa'i dbyangs rngom pa'o// de yang zhal ye shes kyi phyag rgya rnam pa lnga'i bsreg khang du ro rnam pa lngas tshim zhing mchod pa 'brel ba rnam lnga'i tshul dang / gsung dbyangs tshul 'dus byas dang / rang bzhin zung ma 'dres par ston pa'i tshul dang / mche ba bzhi ye shes bzhi'i 'phro 'dus dug bzhi ye shes bzhis gcod pa'i tshul dang / 'brug ltar sgrogs pa'i yan lag drug cu'i dbyangs kyis snyan pa'i mdo sdes go bar sgrogs shing zil gyis gnon pa'i tshul dang rnam par bshad do// thugs kyi rngom pa bzhi la ting nge 'dzin phyag rgya'i rgyan gyi skar tshogs ltar rngom/ phrin las rgya mtsho rgyan gyi dba' rlabs ltar rngom/ yon tan sa gzhi rgyan gyi rtsi shing ltar rngom/ mdzad pa rol mo rgyan gyi gar thabs ltar rngom pa'o// de yang rgya chen po bzhi ni rang bzhin dang rgyan du dbye'o// lhag mthong gi rang bzhin las lhag mthong gi rgyan ma g.yos par snang ba'i tshul dang / zhi gnas kyi rang bzhin las zhi gnas kyi rgyan khyad par du 'byung ba'i tshul dang / zhi gnas kyi rang bzhin bzod pa las lhag mthong gi rgyan gyis phan 'dogs pa'i tshul dang / zhi gnas kyi rang bzhin mi zad ma gol ba las lhag mthong gi rgyan gyis cir yang 'gyur ba'i dga' bskyed pa'i tshul lo// mthu'i rngom pa bzhi la ru tra bcos pa'i gnas rngom/ lha chen gnon pa'i gdan rngom/ khams gsum sgrol ba'i zhing rngom// rtogs 'joms spyod pa'i brtul zhugs rngom/ de yang gnas khyad par can bkra shis shing cis kyang mi tshugs pa'i tshul dang / gnas khyad par can thams cad zil gyis gnon pa'i tshul dang / zhing khyad par can khams gsum yo sgrol ba'i tshul dang / spyod pa khyad par can srid pa'i rtog pa dus gcig tu bcom pa'i tshul lo// rngom tshul sum cu rtsa gnyis bshad do// de la brjid chen po la/ sku che yan lag rags pas brjid che/ grangs mang rkyen dang 'tsham pas brjid che/ bkur 'os gtso bor mthong bas brjid che/ khyad zhugs yid dang 'thad pas brjid che ba ste bzhi'o// de yang chos sku dang mnyam par 'byung ba'i sgo nas sku che/ thugs rje dang mnyam par 'byung ba'i sgo nas sprul rags/ sems 'du byed dang mnyam par 'byung ba'i sgo nas sprul pa grangs mang // smon lam gyi sgo nas rigs dang mthun pa'i rkyen du 'tsham/ spyod lam gyi sgo nas bkur bar 'os/ rigs btsun pa'i sgo nas gtso bor mthong // rang bzhin grub pa'i sgo nas khyad zhugs/ phrin las kyi sgo nas yid dang 'thad/ gsung gi brjid bzhi la gdangs che stong gsum gang bas brjid che/ tshig myur the tsom gcod pas brjid che/ bdag la cher ston snyam pas brjid che/ khyad zhugs yon tan mthong bas brjid che de yang chos skus khyab pa'i sgo nas sgra che/ sgra tha dad pa'i sgo nas stong gsum gang // sgra dbyangs sgo nas kun gyis go bas myur/ nye bar bsgyur ba'i sgo nas the tsom gcod/ byams pa'i sgo nas bdag la gzigs/ thugs rje'i sgo nas nyi tsher ston/ shes pa'i bye brag gi sgo nas khyad zhugs/ tshig gi yon tan gyi sgo nas 'dul/ thugs kyi brjid bzhi la/ yangs pa re dogs med pas brjid che/ gsal ba mtha' gnyis spangs pas brjid che/ thugs rje thugs dam mthar 'byin pas brjid che/ ma rmongs thabs kyis 'dul bas brjid che'o// de yang gnyis med pa'i sgo nas yangs/ spang blang med pa'i sgo nas re dogs med/ lhag mthong gi sgo nas dbu mar gsal/ zhi gnas kyi sgo nas mi 'gyur bas gnyis mtha' spangs/ mdzad pa rgyun mi 'chad pa'i sgo nas thugs rje che/ 'khor ba ci srid bzhugs pa'i sgo nas thugs dam mthar 'byin/ shes rab kyi sgo nas rmongs pa sel/ ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo rnams thabs kyis 'dul/ yon tan gyi brjid pa bzhi la/ med pa zad mi shes pas brjid che/ gcig la 'dod dgur ston pas brjid che/ gnod sbyor phan par 'dod pas brjid che/ thabs mkhas skyon gyis mi gos pas brjid che'o// de yang bdag tu mi 'dzin pa'i sgo nas med/ med pa'i sgo nas zad mi shes/ ye shes kyi sgo nas gcig // sems kyi sgo nas 'dod dgur ston// sems kyi sgo nas gnod par sbyor// grub pa rgyu'i sgo nas phan par mdzad// shes bya'i sgo nas thabs mkhas/ spyod pa'i sgo nas skyon gyis ma gos/ phrin las kyi brjid bzhi la/ mi mnyel nyams phag rol pas brjid che/ 'khor ba yun mi mnyel bar brjid che/ mgon skyabs rgyun du mdzad pas brjid che/ dgongs pa'i don rnams mdzad pas brjid che'o// de yang sgyu mar gyur pa'i sgo nas mi mnyel/ rang bzhin gcig pa'i sgo nas phag tu rol/ spyod pa'i sgo nas 'khor bar yun rings por bzhugs/ bya ba med pa'i sgo nas mi mnyel/ mthu yi sgo nas mgon skyabs che/ dam bcas pa'i sgo nas 'gro don rgyun du mdzad/ rtse gcig gi sgo nas mtha' gnyis kyi skyon dgongs/ nan tan gyi sgo nas bya ba grub// brjid nyi shu dang sgo bzhi bcu ste spyir drug cu'o// de la rin po che sna bdun ni 'khor lo rin po che'i dbang bcus skye ba bzhi la dbang bskur ro// btsun mo rin po ches ni yul gyi rgyal po la mnyes par dbul lo// dmag mi rin po che'i tshul dgus pha rol gyi dpung 'joms so// khyim bdag rin po che'i tshad med pa bzhis rgyal po'i chab srid 'dzin to// glang po rin po che'i stobs bcus pha rol du bdag dang gzhan gyi don byed do// rta rin po che'i myur mgyogs rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhis bgrod pa'i gnas sleb par byed do// yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che ni rnam pa bzhi'i sgo nas sems can gyi re 'dod skong ngo // lung rnam pa gsum ni mi 'da' ba rgyan gyi lung la sogs pa gong du rtsis mgo spyir sbyar bar zad/ de nas 'khor lo rin po che'i dbang bcu ni/ skye bzhi skur ston skye bzhi sgrol mdzad pa// lha mi sdig sbrul mche ba bzhi ru ston// yo byad brid pa'i 'dod yon lnga dang ni// rtog pa gzhom phyir sman lnga dang len rol// ci ltar mos bzhin 'dod dgu gzugs ston pa// gar dbang 'thad dga'i tshul du rol pa mdzad// rdzu 'phrul ba spu'i dbyings nas phra men 'phro// lus ni ci rdzu sems ni cho 'phrul ston// gad rgyangs gdangs ngar sgrogs pa sna tshogs kyis// mche ba zil gnon tha dad chos rnams ston// shes rab thabs ldan spyan gnyis dbu ma'i ngang // dbyings las ma g.yos cir yangs le mkhyen// sems kyi bye brag ting 'dzin tha dad 'phro// bsam gyis mi khyab bzhi la rol pa mdzad// rdo rje sder mo pags pa spu phreng brgyan// 'khor ba ci srid bzhugs pa'i tshe la dbang // lta ba rnam bzhi spyan zur gyis bskul bas// phra men bzhi 'phro phyogs bzhir las bzhi mdzad// smon lam dbang gis drag po skur ston pa// dus mtha'i bskal pa bzhin du bshol du med// de la btsun mo rin po che'i dbang ni/ ma chags rdo rje gzugs kyi yum gyis 'khyud// zhi gnas ting 'dzin mi g.yo yum gyis sbyor// thogs med shugs 'chang don grub yum gyis bskyod// lhag mthong ye shes yum gyis mnyes byed 'bebs// 'byung ba bzhi po rdo rje lha mo ste// bde ba chen po'i sku la mnyes par dbul// dmag mi rin po che yi tshul dgu ni// bsgregs pas 'gro ba shes rab bskyed pa'i tshul// nyam nga med pa'i mdza' spyod dpa' bo'i tshul// gdug rtsub gdos bcad brgyan pas 'jigs pa'i tshul// log par ltar ba zhe gcod gshe ba'i bzhi ni/ chos dbyings med bzhin cir snang ba// mkha' la 'ja' tshon bzhin du rnam par bkram// ye shes rdzu 'phrul chos kyi dbyings rtogs pa// mkha' la nyi shar bzhin du gsal la stong // tshogs gnyis rdzogs pa'i rdzu 'phrul bye brag ni// mkha' dang mnyam pa'i sprin phung bzhin du bdal// sprul pa'i bye brag 'phro ba'i rdzu 'phrul ni// ro la cig car 'babs snod bye brag phye// de la nor bu rin po che'i rang bzhin ni/ 'gro rnams ci ltar 'dod pa'i re 'dod skong // mi zad bdag nyid gter chen nam mkha'i mdog // srid gsum mun nag sel ba'i ye shes sgron// dus gsum rgyun mi 'chad pa'i rin chen phreng // lung gsum ni rtsis mgo spyir sbyar ba yin no// da ni lha rgyud kyi rtogs pa so sor bshad par bya ste/ 'gro rnams ji ltar 'dul zhing gshegs mdzad pa// shes rab nam mkha'i bskal pa dga' rgyud ston// 'joms mdzad pa// zhe sdang rdo rje badzra he ru ka / rin chen dbyig ltar kun skong zhing // bdag med zhi gnas chu yi bskal pas 'khru// nga rgyal tshul gyis nga rgyal 'joms mdzad pa// nga rgyal rdo rje rat+na he ru ka / 'khor ba'i 'dam du pad ltar sku 'khrungs shing // lhag mthong me chen 'bar bas thams cad sreg // 'dod chags tshul gyis 'dod chags 'joms mdzad pa// 'dod chags rdo rje pad+ma he ru ka / phrin las rgya mtshos 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa'i// shes bya thogs med bskal pa'i rlung gis bskyod// phrag dog tshul gyis phrag dog 'joms mdzad pa// phrag dog rdo rje karma he ru ka / sku yi longs ye shes dkar mo'i tshogs// 'gugs mdzad ye shes lnga yi dbyug to can// dran pas rgyud lnga sgrol mdzad zhi bar gzigs// srid gsum 'joms byed dbyug thogs gau rim// sku yi yon tan tshogs sdud rkun mo'i gzigs// nga rgyal 'chi bdag 'joms mdzad bya khra ma// mdzes byed dam tshig rnam dag gsung gi yum// thabs mkhas spyod pas bdag dang gzhan don mdzad// don gyi chos sku ting 'dzin ljags la gtang // 'dod rjes sems can phrin las mtshan ma 'joms// dbu mar ye shes snying rje mi rtog dang // mi g.yo mgon po mnyes mdzad mu ha la// rdo rje gtum mo mtshan ma'i dngos po bcom// thugs rje rngam tshul srid pa thal bar brlag // gnyis la mi gnas mtha' bral dbu mar bsdigs// ha ya grI pa mnyes mdzad tsaN+Da li// phra mor 'bigs pa'i ye shes dbyings su 'phen// 'bigs pa'i ye shes gnad du thugs rjes rdeg // ma khyogs dbu ma chen po'i don ston pa// gzhan gyis mi thub mnyes byed sha ya ti// mtshan ma med pa'i dbyings thos rig pa'i sgra// dbyings nyid rig shes dbyings la nyan pa'i sgra// de la bstan pa gsung gi sgra 'byin pa// bdud rtsir 'khyil ba sha ya ya tis mnyes// bdag rtog log lta'i mtshan ma kun bcom zhing // za byed mche bas skye bzhi rtsad gcad de// sku dang ye shes ma skyes mi dmigs pa// pad+mo 'khyil pa mnyes byed ma ra na// thugs dam dbang gis rnam dag dbyings nas bskul// thugs rje'i shugs kyis 'gro ba gnas nas 'dren// gnyis med mchod bskul dbu ma'i dgyes pa stobs// ma ha ha la mnyes mdzad tsun da ma// bskyod pa'i ye shes sa rnams dus gcig gcod// thugs rje shugs kyis 'gro ba gnas nas spor// thabs dang shes rab bskyod pas mtha' gnyis spor// ba ya ba tis khams gsum hU~M mdzad gnyis// sdug bsngal thugs rjes mi bzod phrin las dpa'// yal bar mi 'dor brtson 'grus shugs kyis brtan// gdod nas don mdzad 'khor ba mthar thug sgrol// de phyir dpa' brtul za byed bya khra ma// sdang mig mi 'gyur thugs rjes zhi la gnon// mthu rtsal rngom brjid 'gyur med bdud dpung bzlog // tsham ngam ral gsigs gdangs ngar 'jig rten 'gengs// de phyir 'gyur med phra men tsa sa ra// rtog pa'i dgra spangs dran pa'i dgon par gnas// 'khrul skyon dri med shes bzhin rdzi mtshor spong // 'gro don dus la bab na thugs rjes 'jug // de phyir 'jug par byed pa'i ha ri na// chos dbyings gnas mal rtog pa'i skyon sel zhing // thugs rje spu ris sprul pa bsam mi khyab// dug gsum 'joms mdzad sha rus khrag la rol// sel byed sprul pas don mdzad d+h+ya ma// yang dag zon chags 'gro don thabs mkhas ldan// mi 'dul zing thub btang snyoms chen por bzhugs// dus la bab nas brtson 'grus shugs dang ldan// de'i phyir mkhas brtson mdzad pa'i rtsa la ma// ye shes dbyings la 'jug pa shes bya za// dbyings nyid shes la 'jug pa nyon mongs za// gnyis med ye shes phrin las 'khor ba za// de phyir za byed bu ka mu ka ba// rigs btsun gnyen por gyur pas thams cad 'dul// phrin las rtsal gyis bdud dpung thams cad 'joms// stong nyid sgra bsgrags mu stegs wa tshogs 'jigs// de phyir 'joms byed rtsa mchog sing ha ma// dbyings la ye shes nyal zhing thugs rje rmi// lhing nag nag po drag po sku ston pa// thugs mchog rnam dag chos nyid dbyings su mkhyen// de phyir rmi byed phra men rik+Sha ma// ye shes thugs rje stobs kyis mtha' gnyis gnon// tsham ngam ral gsigs sprul pas bdud dpung 'joms// las su ci mdzad brtson 'grus stobs kyis rol// de phyir stobs ldan phra men ha k+Sha ma// lhag mthong chos dbyings zhi gnas rlan gyis brgyal// thugs rje 'khor bar smon lam stobs kyis myos// rtog 'joms rdzas la gtsang sme med par rol// de phyir phra men myos byed u ka ra// yid g.yo las can sems par gyur pa ni// ye shes dbang gis thugs rjes 'gro la g.yo// don mdzad god 'brang ye shes dbyings su mkhyen// de phyir tshul khrims chen po kyi kya ma// bsam pa'i dngos po 'dod la 'dun pa ni// dbyings nyid mnyam nyid ye shes mkhyen pa za// thugs rje 'dun pas 'khor ba bag chags sbyong // de phyir phra men za byed don ka ma// dbyings la sems 'dzin yid la byed par 'gyur// ye shes dbyings rtogs drangs pa nyin mo nyal// 'gro mdongs rmongs la thugs rjes mtshan mo ldan// ye shes thugs rjes drangs pa'i u lu ka// brtags pa'i dngos la rtse gcig ting 'dzin 'gyur// mnyam nyid mtha' bral dbyings las mi g.yo ba// rtog ge spyod yul byis pas mi mthong ba// de phyir sbed byed phra men ba ya ta// las 'bras bden la yid ches dad gyur te// mnyam nyid dbyings su ye shes thugs kyis mgyogs// zhi gnas spyan rdzi lhag mthong bgrod tshags chung // de phyir phra men mgyogs byed b+hag shi ta// nges pa'i dngos la 'dzin pa'i mos pa gyur// lhag mthong ye shes dbyings nyid mnyam 'gyur 'dzin// zhi gnas gces par 'dzin pa mi 'phrogs pa// de phyir phra men 'dzin ma tsa ta ma// 'dris pa'i dngos po ma brjed dran par gyur// dbyings dang ye shes gnyis med ma brjed dran// ting 'dzin 'bum phrag lhag mthong so sor gsal// gnyis la ma rmongs zin ma ti ti la// chos rnams 'byed pa'i byed par gyur pa ni// mnyam nyid ngang du log lta sel byed cing // rig pa skyed pas som nyi the tshom gcod// de phyir phra men gsod byed na ku la// 'jug pa rang dbang med pa'i gnyid gyur pa// bstan pa'i chos sgrogs log lta myos byed cing // mnyam dang mi mthun log lta myos byed phyir// thams cad myos byed phra men 'u shi ka / gsum 'dus gcod pa'i reg pa gyur pa ni// phrin las bye brag mang po ci mdzad cing // phyag rgya bzhi po ma skyes dbyings su bros// de phyir phra men 'bros byed ka si ka// 'khor ba'i rdo rje brjod pas mya ngan 'das// chos sku rdo rje brjod pas mtha' gnyis spangs// rjod byed brjod bral don gyi tshig dang bral// de phyir rjod byed badzra ba sha ma// chos nyid rdo rjes mtshan ma'i dngos po bshig // ye shes rdo rjes gzung 'dzin rtog pa bsregs// phyag mtshan rdo rjes dregs pa'i lha bdud bcom// de phyir 'joms byed badzra be ra be// 'chi med bdud rtsi yul sems skye 'gag med// grub pa'i bdud rtsi bsam pa'i 'bras bu thob// thugs rjes 'gro bdud rtsi gtong bla med bsgrub// rtsi mchog ye shes badzra a mr-i ta// ye shes 'phrog byed yon tan rgya mtsho bsgrub// thugs rjes 'phrog byed 'jig rten dbang du sdud// ye shes thugs rjes gnyis med dbang du 'ub// de phyir brlab byed badzra ma ra na// da ni pad+ma dbang chen dang / dbang phyug ma lha rgyud brjod par bya'o// lnga spyan gyis rgyud lnga'i mi dge bcu// ye shes lnga dang so so cis 'dul mkhyen// snyan bcus mi dge bcu yi sdug bsngal gsan// shangs lnga nas byung rigs lnga'i sprul 'phros pas// rgyud lnga'i mgon mdzad brtson ldan rta dbu lnga// dug lnga zhal du shar te rngub mdzad cing // ljags lnga the tshom gcod phyir theg lnga 'chang // skye bzhi las bzhis sgrol mdzad shog bzhis skyod// bcu drug dmyal khams bcu drug phyag gis 'dren// phyogs brgyad 'dul phyir zhabs brgyad khro brgyad bcom// rigs bzhi snod bcud nyi zla 'od dang brdzis// phyogs bzhi rtsal drug dbang phyug yang ches mnan// che ba che ba yang che bla na med// bcu drug zhag gis zla dkyil rdzogs pa lta// tshogs gnyis rdzogs pas bcu drug sa la zhugs// phyogs bzhi dbu lngar 'bar ltar rigs lnga'i dbu// mkhyen pa'i ye shes thugs rjes gzigs// tshogs chen yongs su rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor dang // dbang chen yongs su 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor dang // tshogs chen gnyis rdzogs ye shes lhun grub pa// dkyil 'khor gsum gyis brjid pa'i khro bo rgyal// thugs rje 'dam skyes spyod pa skyon mi gos// mtha' gnyis dbang mdzad pad+ma he ru ka / rngam pa'i tshul gyis srin mo gzugs 'dzin cing // thod rus gdug pa 'bum mar zas su za// srid pa'i sems can chags pa'i snying khrag gsol// dbang drag las mdzad ma bu rak+Sha si// sdug bsngal mya ngan 'das rtogs tshangs pa'i gzugs// tshad med bzhi rdzogs rtags kyi dbu bzhir ldan// zhabs bzhis smra 'don gling bzhir bkra shis brjod// gti mug yid bzhin rin chen pra ma ti// thams cad mnyam pa nyid rtogs rigs mchog ma// ma rig dug gsum 'joms mdzad dpal rtse bsnams// bud med chags tshul dbang mdzad bka' zlog ma// chags pa'i skyon bral te chen re'u tri ma// thams cad sgyu ma bzhin du rtogs mkhyen ma// 'brel ba'i thugs rjes sems can kun la gtogs// phrin las rgya mtsho sgrol ba'i bzhed chen can// 'khor ba'i rgyud gcod drag mo po sna be// 'du phyed mi rtag dril bu'i sgra ltar mkhyen// rtag par gzhon tshul 'khor ba ji srid bzhugs// nyon mongs tha ba 'bigs pa'i mdung thung 'phen// gzhon tshul chags pas dbang mdzad go'u ri// rdo rje las mdzad kun gyi bla na med// lha yi rgyal srid chos la dbang bsgyur zhing // mtshon sbyin brgya mdzad mi dmigs sku dkar mdog // gsod byed rdo rje 'bebs byed in dra ma// byams dang thugs rjes dbang mdzad sku mdog dmar// b+han d+ha snod yangs bcud kyi khrag mtsho la// rngam pa'i zhal du dug gsum za byed ma// sdug bsngal dbyings su skyongs mdzad pi ka lam// sems can gdul thabs khro bo mchog tu mkhyen// mun sel sgron 'bar bdud kyi nad gsos mdzad// 'dam skyes pad ltar 'khor bar sku 'khrungs kyang // chags pa'i skyon bral dbang mdzad a mr-i ta// zhi ba'i las ni gsod pa'i mchog tu mkhyen// zla ltar yon tan cha shas mthar phyin sku// gdung ba'i nad sel 'jig rten sgrol mdzad cing // gtan mchog thams cad stobs byed se'u mya la// dbyug pa 'tshog pa 'dra ba gzhan med mkhyen// thabs kyis ma rmongs phrin las ljang gu'i mdog // nan dbang drag shul 'tshog pa'i dbyug to bsnams// dregs byed spyi nas 'joms mdzad da na ham// log par lta ba 'jigs byed spyan gyi mchog // skye ba 'phrog byed skye rgyun khrag mtsho gsol// las mdzad chags pa gser gyi rked chings can// drag mo rngam tshul glog 'gyu rak+Sha si// phreng ba rgyan gyi nang na mchog tu mdzes// snying rje rgyun skad ba su zhags pa yis// chags med zhing du khams gsum kun 'dren ma// rgyun gyis thugs rjes sgrol mdzad bak+Sha si// 'tshog pa dbyug pas 'chang ba'i mchog tu mkhyen// gtun bus gdug pa ma lus 'joms mdzad ma// yon tan mi zad nor gyi gter 'dzin ma// stong gsum nor gyis rgyas mdzad ral gri ma// ra ro 'dra bar dpa' bo gzhan med mkhyen// chos rnams gnyis med don rtags rtag tu myos// nyon mongs tha ba bzlog pa'i gshol bsnams shing // dge ba'i lo tog skyed mdzad ru ti ram// brtan pa tsam gyis gzhan pham dpa' bo mchog // ma lus gsod byed las la 'jug mdzad cing // bsnyengs pa mi mnga' 'gro don gcig pu spyod// gsod byed 'dra mdzad e ka ra tsa ma// bud med chags pas 'gro ba dbang du byed// thams cad ma lus mgu byed dge ba'i las// 'dod lha'i mda' 'phen srid gsum yid 'phrog ma// thugs rjes zhen pa'i ma no ha ra ma// khrag las zas gzhan med par rtogs mkhyen cing // gdon rnams bsgyur ba'i las mdzad sgo gtong can// mi zad nor gyi gter ldan bum pa 'dzin// sdug bsngal re skong thag thug si ti ka// reg bya'i sems ni rlung gi khams te mchog // srid gsum dbugs kyi srog sbyin tshe 'phel ma// bder gshegs ras rgyus sems can sgrol mdzad cing // khams gsum gnas nas skyon mdzad pa ya be// snyigs ma lnga ldan lnga brgya'i tha ma la// srid gsum 'khor ba'i sems can gdul dka' ba// gsad pa nyid la las kyis 'dul bar mdzad// sdug bsngal dbyings su gsol mdzad ma ra cad gsod byed dam nyams 'chi bdag mdzad// dam tshig bsrung ba'i 'chi bdag zlog mdzad cing // lung gi dur khrod dbang mdzad dza mun ti// 'jigs las lhags pa'i grags ni gzhan med mkhyen// stong phrag brgyad cu grags la mnga' mdzad cing // sna chen glang sna bdud rtsi gi'u wang mthong // sdug bsngal nad gsos mdzad pa'i bu ta ma// chu las lhag pa'i nor ni gzhan med mkhyen// nor gyi tshogs rnams ma po bsnams// thugs rje shugs kyis 'dren mdzad lcags kyu bsnams// 'khor bar thugs rjes shar ba'i ka ma la// chags pa'i thugs rjes don mdzad ra mgo can// byams pa'i zhags pa 'khor ba'i rgyud 'dzin cing // gang la ci 'dul de la des ston pa// yon tan tshogs rdzogs re skong tsa ka lam// ston pa'i bka' dang rang gi dam bca' gnyis// mi 'da' ma grub rab tu brtan par bzhugs// dam tshig sgrog gis sems can rje las thabs dang shes rab kyi byang chub kyi sems kyi dbang 'di bka' stsal to// dkyil 'khor 'dom gang gru bzhi la dbus su pad+ma 'dab ma brgyad/ pad+ma'i lte ba la rag ta'i maN+Dal byas te/ dbus su badzra he ru ka / shar du bud d+ha he ru ka / lhor rad na he ru ka / nub tu pad+ma he ru ka / byang du karma he ru ka / mtshams bzhir khro mo dbang phyug ma bzhi// de'i phyi rim snam bu la go'u ri ma brgyad// de'i phyi rim la sing ha ma brgyad// sgo bzhi dang sgo khyud dang bcas pa// zhing gi rgyal mtshan// ras chen gyi 'phan gdugs/ tsit+ta'i thog // maM sa'i bla res de nas bcom ldan 'das thabs dang shes rab gnyis su med pa'i byang chub kyi sems yum gyi sku la bstims te// yum kun du bzang mos rang gis mtha' la byang chub kyi sems blangs te/ nyid las mi gzhan pa'i 'khor rnams dbang bskur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // byang chub sems nyid sgom pa'i dbang // dbyings dang dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor 'dir// sems nyid rtogs pa'i thig btab ste// de ru slob ma bskur bar bya// chos rnams thams cad brtag par dka'// brjod pa'i tha snyad kun las 'das// da ltar sa gsum gnon pa ni// sems can nang na mi yin te// sangs rgyas mis ni bsgrub thag nye// byang chub sems de'i don rtogs nas// 'bras bu yang dag mngon du 'char// de las kyang ni ma gtogs pa// de las sangs rgyas gzhan na med// sems nyid dngos po de las med// bstan cing yang ni rtogs par dka'// bsgom pa'i dngos gzhi'ang de las med// sems kyis brtag par dka' na yang // tshig gis 'di yin bstan dka' zhes// sangs rgyas byang chub sems nyid 'di// de ring khyod la bskur bar bya// bo d+hi tsit+ta hU~M/ phyi yi tshul du rtogs 'gyur na// sems la srid pa thams cad chub par 'gyur// nang gi tshul du rtogs 'gyur na// sems la sku gsung thugs kyang 'phrugs par gnas// gsang ba'i tshul du snang ba thams cad ni// yum chen kun du bzang mo zhes kyang bya// sems ni snang ba shar ba'i ye shes yin// gnyis su med par rtogs na chos kyi sku// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// badzra tsit+ta hU~M/ mngon pa'i sangs rgyas che ba yum chen kun du bzang // bdag nyid chen po sangs rgyas kun du bzang po ni// yab yum gnyis su med par gyur pa las// byang chub sems nyid bde ba chen po yin// chos kyi dbyings su sangs rgyas bde ba chen po ni// yum dang sems nyid gnyis su med pa yin// rdo rje sems ni ye nas mi 'gyur te// skye 'gag med pa'i sems nyid don yin te// sems dpa' yi ni bdud bzhi med pa'i don// kun du khyab cing bdal ba dpag tu med// thams cad man ngag la ni thams cad rten// gdod nas 'tshang ni rgya ba'i che bar gsungs// phyi ni snod kyi 'jig rten rtogs 'gyur na// 'byung ba lnga las sangs rgyas gzhan na med// nang ni bcud kyi 'jig rten rtogs 'gyur na// sems las ma gtogs sangs rgyas gzhan na med// byang chub sems kyis dbang bskur ro// bsdu ba'i gnas su nges pa med ces bya// rang 'byung ye shes nyid kyang tshig gi mtha' las 'das// sems la dngos po med cing gzung du med// gnas ni yum gyi b+ha ga ya ti ste// rnam par mi rtog chos nyid stong par gsal// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// rig pa rnyed pa dag la shin tu gsal// byang chub sems kyi dngos gzhi ma gtogs pa// sangs rgyas gzhan na med ces 'byung ba yang // mi rtog pa'i lta ba mi bslad pa'i ye shes te// mi gtong ba'i spyod pa mi 'gyur ba'i sems nyid yin// mi 'da' ba'i dam tshig mi 'bral ba'i gzungs// mi g.yo ba yi chos nyid dbyings dag pas// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// mnyam par shes pa sangs rgyas kun gyi rje// mtho ris srin mo na rag dmyal ba kun// mnyam pa'i don dang rig pa gnyis med pas// 'di dang phyi ma'i don du bsgom par bya// byang chub sems kyis de yang gsang ba'i gnas su rtogs par bya// kun gzhi yid dang rnam shes yid dang gsum// gsang ba'i mdzod gsum yin pas bskur bar bya// de la sems kyi gzugs ni ci 'dra ba// tsit+ta'i dbyings nas 'od ni tshon gang gsal bar bsgom// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// rtag pa chen po rnam snang mdzad// mi bskyod pa ni sems kyi mchog // bdag gi lus ni rtag pa ste// bdag gi gsung ni 'gyur ba yin// bdag gi sems ni mi bskyod pa// sems nyid dus gsum 'gyur ba med par gsungs// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// thig le chen po dgu yi lung bstan pa// man ngag gnyer chen rnam shes rdzogs// sangs rgyas kun gyi rje btsan bskal par mi nyams rdul tsam med// rig pa'i rgyal po rdo rje rang dbang las// gzhan nas sangs rgyas btsal gyur kyang // btsal kyang rgyal ba mi rnyed do// thams cad 'gyur med byang chub sems dpa' las// ma gtogs gzhan na med ces bya bar gsungs// byang chub sems nyid mnyam par khyab bdal te// bdag dang gzhan du med par rtogs pa la// de ltar sus rtogs skyes bu gcig pu yin// lhun gyis rdzogs pa zhes kyang de la bya// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// dran pa'i sems can sems kyi rang bzhin ni// dkar 'tsher snum la 'dril bas byang chub sems// mdzangs pa zin po sems shes de la bya// blun po byol song sems ni na bun dud pas 'dres// sems gnas phung po tsit+ta'i dbyings dkyil na// 'od kyi thig le dkar 'tsher gnas pa ni// nga dang bdag tu 'dzin pa'i sems de ni// ti dang ra dang nas btags zhabs 'khyud rnams// gu gu zla tshes dag tu gnas gyur te// mi las sangs rgyas dag tu gnas bsgyur nas// dus gsum sangs rgyas kun gyi thugs kyi sa bon 'di// bdag gis ma yengs brjed bral med par 'di bsgoms na// sangs rgyas 'bras bu yang dag byang chub sems// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// nyams pa'i chad pa byung ba la// mgon chun de las gzhan med do// rnal 'byor dam nyams gzhan gyis mi skongs kyis// bdag gi sems nyid kun tu bzang po'i ngang gyur na// bya tsa dang ni bral zhing 'das pa yin// 'khor ba dang ni mya ngan 'das pa yang // nga dang bdag tu 'dzin pa dbyer med mnyam pa chen po dang // de la sangs rgyas gang nas btsal kyang rgyal bas rnyed par ma gsungs so// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// glang po dpal gyi thugs ka nas// lcags kyi zer chen bzhi 'phros te// glang po dpal chen he ru ka'i// lus ngag yid gsum sku gsung thugs kyi dkyil 'khor las// 'od zer dgu 'phros gdug pa ma lus bcom// 'gro ba mtha' dag rnams kyi don byas te// bdag gi rnam par shes pa'i tshogs brgyad kyang // kun gzhi snying la 'dus pa'i he ru ka// de ltar lags pas rtogs na byang chub sems// gang nas btsal kyang rnyed par mi 'gyur te// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// bdag med khams kyi snod gang du// rgya che gsal ba'i khams bkang ste// re dogs med par phung 'gro yang // nyam nga med par lam gyi mchog // gza' gtad med pas don du bde// de bas rang sems bgrod pa'i sa// byang chub sems ni yangs shing rgya che ste// de bas bdag gis lus rtogs na// snod bcud la sogs rtogs pa'i skyes mchog rnams// shes gsal blo ldan rnams la ye nas rnyed pa gsal// bla ma'i rgyud mchog de la yod ces gsungs te rdzogs// rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems kyis dbang bskur ro// bsgoms pas rnyed par mi 'gyur ma bsgoms stong bral med// thugs nas zhal du byung ba 'gro ba'i don du gsungs// rna rgyud ston pas thugs brtol te// lus dang sems las ma gtogs bsgom du med// bsgoms nas sems nyid gzhan nas btsal yang rnyed par ma gsungs so// dus gsum rgyal bas ye nas ma bcos te// rang sems gdod nas ma skyes chos kyi sku// chos nyid bsgom par bya ba gang yang med// man ngag shes rab sbyin chen des gsungs pas// lus dang sems las ma gtogs na// bdag gi sku gsung thugs la tshang bar gnas// gal te brjod pa'i mtha' bzhi yod na ni// don rdzogs sgom pa po yang yod par gyur// lus sems skye ba med bden pas// bsgom du med par 'jog pa gang // don kun rdzogs shing chub par der gnas so// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// zla gsang dkar dmar rlung ka lci// zla ba shes rab gsal ba thabs chen te// thig le byang chub sems nyid dkar la 'tsher ba yi// dmar ba yug gi rak+ta byang chub sems// rlung la shor du mi rtsal thig le sgrom du sba// de las ma gtogs sangs rgyas gzhan na med// man ngag tshul du zla ba'i gzugs yin te// gsang ba'i tshul du yid kyi rnam shes nyid kyang zla ba yin// thig le sems kyi rang bzhin snum la 'dril// man ngag len par byed pas sems kyi thig le yin// sems las ma gtogs sangs rgyas gzhan na med// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// rang 'byung che ba'i ye shes mi 'gyur la// chos nyid rang gis gnas pa'i rang bzhin la// dmigs bral ting 'dzin rgya mtshor rab sprul te// yid ni 'phags pa'i lam ni gnas pa ni// phra zhing zab pa bstan dka' rgyal ba'i sku// dran pa byed pa'i rtsol dang srog chags gsum// kun gzhi pad+ma'i yig 'bru gsal bar byed// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// rgyu ni skye ba med pas rnam par dag // 'bras bu 'gags pa med pas byang chub sems// byang chub sems de skye med ye shes dbyings// skye med mi 'gyur mi shigs rdo rje'i don// sems la rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu bsgom// byang chub sems kyis deng 'dir dbang bskur ro// 'byung ba chen po bcom ldan 'das// nam mkha' rdo rje snang ba ston pa'i sangs rgyas so// sa rdo rje chos nyid ye nas gnas pa'i sangs rgyas so// me rdo rje chos nyid rin po che'i sangs rgyas so// chu rdo rje snying rje chen pos brlan pa'i sangs rgyas so// rlung rdo rje 'dod pa sgrol ba'i sangs rgyas so// 'byung ba bcom ldan 'das kyis dbang bskur ro// dngos grub stsol ba rnam gnyis te// nges pa'i lung dang rang bzhin no// chos kyi dbyings las mnga' brnyes nas// gang ltar bsgrub kyang dbyings kyi don// chos kyi dbyings la 'char ba dang // dbang chen dbang sgyur 'chi ba med// sprul pa kun du bzang po nyid// sgrib dang 'chi bar mi 'gyur ro// byang chub sems kyis dbang bskur ro// lhun gyis grub pa'i dbang chen ni// de yang sa gser zla ba med// gser dang 'dra ba'i byang chub sems// byang chub sems ni sa zhes bya// zla ba me dang 'dra ba yin// byang chub sems nyid kun du bzang // gsal zhing dro la nyon mongs sreg // byang chub sems kyis dbang bskur ro// don ni dbyings dang ye shes yin// yab yum gnyis med rol pa yi// rak+ta byang chub sems dkyil na// ma skyes rdzogs pa'i he ru ka / sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rgyud// yon tan phrin las rdzogs mdzad pa// gsang ba'i don gyis dbang bskur ro// gsang ba yum chen kun du bzang // rak+ta byang chub sems dkyil na// ma hA su kha'i dkyil 'khor dbyings// sems kyi thig les thig btab ste// dkyil 'khor zlum po 'khyil ba la// chos kyi dbyings las spros pa'i sku// don gyi dbyings nas lha dang lha mo dgod// nges pa'i don gyis dbang bskur ro// nga dang rang bzhin bdag nyid chen po ba'i don ma bgyis pa mthol zhing bshags// le lo gnyid kyi dbang du gyur pas na// bsgom dang bsgrub la g.yel ba mthol zhing bshags// ser sna 'jur 'gegs dbang du gyur pas na// mchod pa lo zla 'das pa mthol zhing bshags// nga rgyal khengs sems dbang du bsdus pa na// slob dpon sku ma mnyes pa mthol zhing bshags// brtse gdung chung ba'i dbang du gyur pas na// grogs mched thugs dang 'gal ba mthol zhing bshags// za rog ngan pa'i dbang du gyur pas na// phud dang lhag mar gyur pa mthol zhing bshags// phud dang lhag ma nyams pa'i skyon dbang gis// phud nyul thugs dang 'gal ba mthol zhing bshags// phud nyul thugs dang 'gal ba'i skyon dbang gis// mkha' 'gro bka' chad gnas su gyur pa mthol zhing bshags// sgrol ba'i dus su snying rje chung ba yis// sems can gnas ma stobs pa mthol zhing bshags// nyon mongs gnas ma stobs pa'i skyon dbang gis// yun gyi sgrib par gyur pa mthol zhing bshags// sbyor ba'i dus su ting 'dzin ma gsal bas// gzungs ma thugs dang 'gal ba'i skyon dbang gis// chags shing 'khor ba'i gnas su mthol zhing bshags// bshags nas sku gsung thugs kyi dngos grub stsol// de skad ces bzod pa phul nas bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang tshangs pa gnang ste/ bka' dam pa 'di yang nas yang du rdo rje chos kyi sdud pa po la gtad do// de nas rdo rje chos kyis bka' dam pa 'di ma chags pa'i dbang gis bka' bzhin byas so// de nas 'khor de dag thal mo sbyar nas rjes su yi rang ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// bcom ldan 'das he ru ka rol pa las yongs su gtad pa'i le'u ste bcu bdun pa'o// // de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang / lha dang / klu dang / lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten yi rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// gsang ba'i snying po zab mo mchog dpal snying rje rol pa'i rgyud rdzogs // // rgya gar gyi lots+tsha ba mkhas par lobs pa bal po shrI kIr tis gtan la phab ste/ skad gsar pas bsgyur nas sog po mchog gi snying po dang / an bkra shis dang / bal po bzang bkra shis rgya mtshos yon bdag bgyis nas mang yul byams sprin gtsug lag khang gi ya thog gi dbu rtser shin tu gsang ste/ skad gsal bar bsgyur ro//
